## Task 17: accounts:add and accounts:remove for OAuth + revocation

**Files:**
- Create: `electron/auth/accountHandlers.ts`
- Create: `electron/auth/accountHandlers.test.ts`
- Modify: `electron/main.ts` (remove inline handlers at lines 340–361 and 407–415, add import + call)

**Spec references:** D9.5, D11.1

The existing `accounts:add` handler at `electron/main.ts:340` and `accounts:remove` at `electron/main.ts:407` are extracted to a new module and extended. `accounts:add` gains an optional `oauth` field (OAuth insert path: `auth_type='oauth2'`, no password). `accounts:remove` gains a pre-delete best-effort Google token revocation (5-second timeout). Microsoft is intentionally skipped per D11.1 — the Graph `revokeSignInSessions` endpoint is nuclear. A code comment documents this in-source.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing tests**

Create `electron/auth/accountHandlers.test.ts`:

```ts
import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';

const {
    mockIpcMainHandle, mockEncryptData,
    mockImapEngineStartAccount, mockImapEngineDisconnectAccount,
    mockGetAuthTokenManager, mockPersistInitialTokens,
    mockGetOAuthCredential, mockRevokeRefreshToken,
    mockDbRun, mockDbGet, mockDbPrepare, mockLogDebug,
} = vi.hoisted(() => ({
    mockIpcMainHandle: vi.fn(),
    mockEncryptData: vi.fn(() => Buffer.from('enc')),
    mockImapEngineStartAccount: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
    mockImapEngineDisconnectAccount: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
    mockGetAuthTokenManager: vi.fn(),
    mockPersistInitialTokens: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
    mockGetOAuthCredential: vi.fn(),
    mockRevokeRefreshToken: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
    mockDbRun: vi.fn(),
    mockDbGet: vi.fn(),
    mockDbPrepare: vi.fn(() => ({ get: mockDbGet, run: mockDbRun, all: vi.fn() })),
    mockLogDebug: vi.fn(),
}));

vi.mock('electron', () => ({ ipcMain: { handle: mockIpcMainHandle } }));
vi.mock('../crypto.js', () => ({ encryptData: mockEncryptData, decryptData: vi.fn(() => 'dec') }));
vi.mock('../imap.js', () => ({
    imapEngine: {
        startAccount: mockImapEngineStartAccount,
        disconnectAccount: mockImapEngineDisconnectAccount,
        stopController: vi.fn(),
    },
}));
vi.mock('../auth/tokenManager.js', () => ({ getAuthTokenManager: mockGetAuthTokenManager }));
vi.mock('../db.js', () => ({
    getDatabase: vi.fn(() => ({ prepare: mockDbPrepare })),
    getOAuthCredential: mockGetOAuthCredential,
}));
vi.mock('../oauth/google.js', () => ({ revokeRefreshToken: mockRevokeRefreshToken }));
vi.mock('../logger.js', () => ({ logDebug: mockLogDebug }));

function getHandler(ch: string): ((_e: unknown, ...a: unknown[]) => Promise<unknown>) | undefined {
    return mockIpcMainHandle.mock.calls.find(([c]) => c === ch)?.[1] as never;
}

const OAUTH_FIELD = {
    provider: 'google' as const, accessToken: 'at', refreshToken: 'rt',
    expiresAt: 9999999999000, scope: 'https://mail.google.com/', tokenType: 'Bearer',
};

await import('./accountHandlers.js');

describe('accounts:add — OAuth path', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
        vi.clearAllMocks();
        mockGetAuthTokenManager.mockReturnValue({ persistInitialTokens: mockPersistInitialTokens });
    });

    it('legacy path: encryptData called, persistInitialTokens NOT called', async () => {
        const h = getHandler('accounts:add')!;
        await h(null, { email: 'u@example.com', provider: 'gmail', password: 'pw' });
        expect(mockEncryptData).toHaveBeenCalledWith('pw');
        expect(mockPersistInitialTokens).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('oauth path: encryptData NOT called, persistInitialTokens called with accountId', async () => {
        const h = getHandler('accounts:add')!;
        const r = await h(null, { email: 'u@gmail.com', provider: 'gmail', password: '', oauth: OAUTH_FIELD }) as Record<string, unknown>;
        expect(r.id).toBeDefined();
        expect(mockEncryptData).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
        expect(mockPersistInitialTokens).toHaveBeenCalledOnce();
        const [calledId, calledProvider] = mockPersistInitialTokens.mock.calls[0];
        expect(typeof calledId).toBe('string');
        expect(calledProvider).toBe('google');
    });

    it('oauth path: imapEngine.startAccount called regardless of auth path', async () => {
        const h = getHandler('accounts:add')!;
        await h(null, { email: 'u@gmail.com', provider: 'gmail', password: '', oauth: OAUTH_FIELD });
        expect(mockImapEngineStartAccount).toHaveBeenCalledOnce();
    });

    it('oauth path: returns { success: false } when persistInitialTokens throws', async () => {
        mockPersistInitialTokens.mockRejectedValueOnce(new Error('DB error'));
        const h = getHandler('accounts:add')!;
        const r = await h(null, { email: 'u@gmail.com', provider: 'gmail', password: '', oauth: OAUTH_FIELD }) as Record<string, unknown>;
        expect(r.success).toBe(false);
        expect(r.error).toBeDefined();
    });
});

describe('accounts:remove — OAuth revocation (D11.1)', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
        vi.clearAllMocks();
        mockGetAuthTokenManager.mockReturnValue({ getDecryptedRefreshToken: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue('rt-raw') });
    });

    it('Google: revokeRefreshToken called before DB delete', async () => {
        mockGetOAuthCredential.mockReturnValue({ accountId: 'acc1', provider: 'google', refreshTokenEncrypted: 'enc_rt' });
        const h = getHandler('accounts:remove')!;
        await h(null, 'acc1');
        expect(mockRevokeRefreshToken).toHaveBeenCalledOnce();
        const revokeOrder = mockRevokeRefreshToken.mock.invocationCallOrder[0];
        const deleteOrder = mockDbRun.mock.invocationCallOrder[mockDbRun.mock.invocationCallOrder.length - 1];
        expect(revokeOrder).toBeLessThan(deleteOrder);
    });

    it('Microsoft: revokeRefreshToken NOT called (D11.1 nuclear risk)', async () => {
        mockGetOAuthCredential.mockReturnValue({ accountId: 'ms1', provider: 'microsoft_personal' });
        const h = getHandler('accounts:remove')!;
        await h(null, 'ms1');
        expect(mockRevokeRefreshToken).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('Google revocation failure: DB delete still proceeds, error logged with [OAUTH]', async () => {
        mockGetOAuthCredential.mockReturnValue({ accountId: 'fail1', provider: 'google', refreshTokenEncrypted: 'enc' });
        mockRevokeRefreshToken.mockRejectedValueOnce(new Error('network timeout'));
        const h = getHandler('accounts:remove')!;
        const r = await h(null, 'fail1') as Record<string, unknown>;
        expect(r.success).toBe(true);
        expect(mockLogDebug).toHaveBeenCalledWith(expect.stringContaining('[OAUTH]'));
    });

    it('password account (no oauth row): delete proceeds, no revocation call', async () => {
        mockGetOAuthCredential.mockReturnValue(null);
        const h = getHandler('accounts:remove')!;
        const r = await h(null, 'pw-acc') as Record<string, unknown>;
        expect(r.success).toBe(true);
        expect(mockRevokeRefreshToken).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Create `electron/auth/accountHandlers.ts`**

```ts
// Phase 2 OAuth extensions to accounts:add and accounts:remove (D9.5, D11.1).
//
// accounts:add — optional oauth field triggers OAuth insert path:
//   auth_type='oauth2', password_encrypted=NULL, persistInitialTokens called.
//   Legacy password path (no oauth field) is byte-for-byte unchanged.
//
// accounts:remove — best-effort Google token revocation (5s timeout) before
//   DB DELETE. Microsoft intentionally skipped per D11.1: Graph
//   revokeSignInSessions is nuclear (revokes ALL tokens for the user across
//   every app, not just ours). Local oauth_credentials row deleted by FK CASCADE.

import { ipcMain } from 'electron';
import crypto from 'node:crypto';
import { getDatabase, getOAuthCredential } from '../db.js';
import { encryptData } from '../crypto.js';
import { logDebug } from '../logger.js';
import { imapEngine } from '../imap.js';
import { getAuthTokenManager } from '../auth/tokenManager.js';
import { revokeRefreshToken as googleRevokeToken } from '../oauth/google.js';
import type { TokenProvider } from '../auth/tokenManager.js';

export function registerAccountHandlers(): void {

    ipcMain.handle('accounts:add', async (_event, account: {
        email: string; provider: string; password: string;
        display_name?: string; imap_host?: string; imap_port?: number;
        smtp_host?: string; smtp_port?: number; signature_html?: string;
        oauth?: {
            provider: TokenProvider;
            accessToken: string; refreshToken: string;
            expiresAt: number; scope: string; tokenType: string;
        };
    }) => {
        const id = crypto.randomUUID();
        const db = getDatabase();
        try {
            if (account.oauth) {
                // OAuth insert path: no password column, auth_type='oauth2'.
                db.prepare(
                    `INSERT INTO accounts
                        (id, email, provider, password_encrypted, auth_type, auth_state,
                         display_name, imap_host, imap_port, smtp_host, smtp_port, signature_html)
                     VALUES (?, ?, ?, NULL, 'oauth2', 'ok', ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`
                ).run(
                    id, account.email, account.provider,
                    account.display_name ?? null, account.imap_host ?? null,
                    account.imap_port ?? 993, account.smtp_host ?? null,
                    account.smtp_port ?? 587,
                    account.signature_html ? account.signature_html.slice(0, 10_000) : null
                );
                await getAuthTokenManager().persistInitialTokens(id, account.oauth.provider, {
                    accessToken: account.oauth.accessToken,
                    refreshToken: account.oauth.refreshToken,
                    expiresAt: account.oauth.expiresAt,
                    scope: account.oauth.scope,
                    tokenType: account.oauth.tokenType,
                    providerAccountEmail: account.email,
                    providerAccountId: account.email,
                });
            } else {
                // Legacy password path — unchanged from pre-Phase-2 behavior.
                const encrypted = encryptData(account.password).toString('base64');
                db.prepare(
                    `INSERT INTO accounts
                        (id, email, provider, password_encrypted, display_name,
                         imap_host, imap_port, smtp_host, smtp_port, signature_html)
                     VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`
                ).run(
                    id, account.email, account.provider, encrypted,
                    account.display_name ?? null, account.imap_host ?? null,
                    account.imap_port ?? 993, account.smtp_host ?? null,
                    account.smtp_port ?? 465,
                    account.signature_html ? account.signature_html.slice(0, 10_000) : null
                );
            }

            imapEngine.startAccount(id).catch((err) => {
                logDebug(`Post-add IMAP sync error: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`);
            });
            return { id };
        } catch (err) {
            const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
            logDebug(`[OAUTH] accounts:add error: ${msg.slice(0, 500)}`);
            return { success: false, error: msg.slice(0, 300) };
        }
    });

    ipcMain.handle('accounts:remove', async (_event, accountId: string) => {
        const db = getDatabase();

        // D11.1: best-effort pre-delete revocation for Google OAuth accounts.
        const oauthCred = getOAuthCredential(db, accountId);
        if (oauthCred !== null) {
            if (oauthCred.provider === 'google') {
                try {
                    const mgr = getAuthTokenManager();
                    const refreshToken = await Promise.race([
                        mgr.getDecryptedRefreshToken(accountId),
                        new Promise<never>((_, rej) => setTimeout(() => rej(new Error('revocation timeout (5s)')), 5_000)),
                    ]);
                    await Promise.race([
                        googleRevokeToken(refreshToken),
                        new Promise<never>((_, rej) => setTimeout(() => rej(new Error('revocation timeout (5s)')), 5_000)),
                    ]);
                    logDebug(`[OAUTH] Revoked Google refresh token for account ${accountId}`);
                } catch (revokeErr) {
                    const msg = revokeErr instanceof Error ? revokeErr.message : String(revokeErr);
                    logDebug(`[OAUTH] Google revocation failed for ${accountId} (non-blocking): ${msg.slice(0, 300)}`);
                    // Intentional: revocation failure does NOT block local delete per D11.1.
                }
            } else {
                // Microsoft: intentionally no server-side revocation per D11.1.
                // Graph revokeSignInSessions is nuclear — revokes ALL tokens for the
                // user across every registered app, not just ours. Local row is
                // removed by FK CASCADE when the accounts row is deleted below.
                logDebug(`[OAUTH] Skipping server-side revocation for Microsoft account ${accountId} per D11.1`);
            }
        }

        try {
            await imapEngine.disconnectAccount(accountId);
        } catch (err) {
            logDebug(`IMAP disconnect error during account removal: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`);
        }
        db.prepare('DELETE FROM accounts WHERE id = ?').run(accountId);
        return { success: true };
    });
}
```

In `electron/main.ts`:
1. Remove the inline `ipcMain.handle('accounts:add', ...)` block (lines 340–361).
2. Remove the inline `ipcMain.handle('accounts:remove', ...)` block (lines 407–415).
3. Add import and call:

```ts
// Import:
import { registerAccountHandlers } from './auth/accountHandlers.js';

// Call (inside setupIpc, after db is initialized):
registerAccountHandlers();
```

```bash
git commit -m "$(cat <<'EOF'

Phase 2 D9.5, D11.1: accounts:add accepts an optional oauth field
for OAuth insert path (auth_type='oauth2', no password, calls
persistInitialTokens). Legacy password path byte-for-byte unchanged.

accounts:remove calls google.revokeRefreshToken (5s timeout,
best-effort) before DB DELETE for Google OAuth accounts. Microsoft
intentionally skipped per D11.1 — Graph revokeSignInSessions is
nuclear and would revoke all tokens across every app for the user.
FK CASCADE handles local oauth_credentials cleanup for both providers.

Handlers extracted to electron/auth/accountHandlers.ts for testability.

tolerance, and Microsoft skip behavior.
EOF
```

## Task 18: preload.ts channel allowlist update

**Files:**
- Modify: `electron/preload.ts`
- Create: `electron/preload.test.ts`

**Spec references:** D9.6

Five new invoke channels and one on-channel are added to `electron/preload.ts`. A typed `auth` sub-object is added to the `contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld` call. The preload builds as CJS `.cjs` (Electron sandbox requirement); Vitest runs in ESM mode and cannot execute the CJS artifact. Tests verify the allowlist and typed API shape by importing the TypeScript source with a mocked `electron` module.

- [ ] **Step 1: Verify no existing `electron/preload.test.ts`**

Run: `ls electron/preload.test.ts 2>/dev/null || echo "NOT FOUND"`

Expected: NOT FOUND.

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing tests**

Create `electron/preload.test.ts`:

```ts
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';

// The preload module calls contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld at evaluation time.
// Mock electron before importing so the call is captured.
vi.mock('electron', () => ({
    ipcRenderer: { invoke: vi.fn(), on: vi.fn(), removeListener: vi.fn() },
    contextBridge: { exposeInMainWorld: vi.fn() },
}));

const { contextBridge } = await import('electron');
await import('../electron/preload.js');

const api = (contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld as ReturnType<typeof vi.fn>)
    .mock.calls[0]?.[1] as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;

const invoke = api?.invoke as ((ch: string, ...a: unknown[]) => void) | undefined;
const on = api?.on as ((ch: string, cb: () => void) => void) | undefined;
const auth = api?.auth as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;

describe('preload.ts Phase 2 OAuth channel allowlist', () => {
    it('auth:start-oauth-flow is in the invoke allowlist', () => {
        expect(() => invoke?.('auth:start-oauth-flow', {})).not.toThrow();
    });
    it('auth:start-reauth-flow is in the invoke allowlist', () => {
        expect(() => invoke?.('auth:start-reauth-flow', {})).not.toThrow();
    });
    it('auth:cancel-flow is in the invoke allowlist', () => {
        expect(() => invoke?.('auth:cancel-flow')).not.toThrow();
    });
    it('auth:flow-status is in the invoke allowlist', () => {
        expect(() => invoke?.('auth:flow-status')).not.toThrow();
    });
    it('auth:get-state is in the invoke allowlist', () => {
        expect(() => invoke?.('auth:get-state', {})).not.toThrow();
    });
    it('unknown auth channel is blocked', () => {
        expect(() => invoke?.('auth:unknown-channel')).toThrow(/not allowed/i);
    });
    it('auth:needs-reauth is in the on-channel allowlist', () => {
        expect(() => on?.('auth:needs-reauth', () => {})).not.toThrow();
    });
    it('auth namespace exposes typed methods', () => {
        expect(typeof auth?.startOAuthFlow).toBe('function');
        expect(typeof auth?.startReauthFlow).toBe('function');
        expect(typeof auth?.cancelFlow).toBe('function');
        expect(typeof auth?.flowStatus).toBe('function');
        expect(typeof auth?.getState).toBe('function');
        expect(typeof auth?.onNeedsReauth).toBe('function');
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Implement the allowlist update in `electron/preload.ts`**

**4a.** Add to `ALLOWED_INVOKE_CHANNELS` before the `] as const` at line 164:

```ts
  // Phase 2: OAuth flows
  'auth:start-oauth-flow',
  'auth:start-reauth-flow',
  'auth:cancel-flow',
  'auth:flow-status',
  'auth:get-state',
```

**4b.** Add to `ALLOWED_ON_CHANNELS` before the `] as const` at line 183:

```ts
  // Phase 2: OAuth re-auth notification (main → renderer)
  'auth:needs-reauth',
```

**4c.** Add the `auth` typed namespace to `contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('electronAPI', { ... })` after the existing `on` method:

```ts
  auth: {
    startOAuthFlow(params: { provider: 'google' | 'microsoft'; presetId: string }) {
      return ipcRenderer.invoke('auth:start-oauth-flow', params);
    },
    startReauthFlow(params: { accountId: string }) {
      return ipcRenderer.invoke('auth:start-reauth-flow', params);
    },
    cancelFlow() {
      return ipcRenderer.invoke('auth:cancel-flow');
    },
    flowStatus() {
      return ipcRenderer.invoke('auth:flow-status');
    },
    getState(params: { accountId: string }) {
      return ipcRenderer.invoke('auth:get-state', params);
    },
    onNeedsReauth(callback: (payload: { accountId: string }) => void) {
      const handler = (_event: Electron.IpcRendererEvent, payload: { accountId: string }) =>
        callback(payload);
      ipcRenderer.on('auth:needs-reauth', handler);
      return () => { ipcRenderer.removeListener('auth:needs-reauth', handler); };
    },
  },
```

```bash
feat(preload): extend channel allowlist for Phase 2 OAuth IPC

Phase 2 D9.6: five new invoke channels + one on-channel added to
electron/preload.ts:

ALLOWED_INVOKE_CHANNELS: auth:start-oauth-flow, auth:start-reauth-flow,
  auth:cancel-flow, auth:flow-status, auth:get-state
ALLOWED_ON_CHANNELS: auth:needs-reauth (main→renderer reauth badge)

New window.electronAPI.auth namespace with typed methods (startOAuthFlow,
startReauthFlow, cancelFlow, flowStatus, getState, onNeedsReauth).

and auth namespace shape via mocked contextBridge introspection. Full
CJS execution not tested — Vitest ESM cannot execute the .cjs artifact;
TypeScript compile-time checking is the primary safety net.

)"
```
## Task 19: OAuthSignInButton component

**Files:**
- Create: `src/components/OAuthSignInButton.tsx`
- Create: `src/components/OAuthSignInButton.module.css`
- Create: `src/components/OAuthSignInButton.test.tsx`

**Spec references:** D2.1, D2.2

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test first**

Create `src/components/OAuthSignInButton.test.tsx`:

```tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent, waitFor } from '@testing-library/react';
import userEvent from '@testing-library/user-event';

vi.mock('react-i18next', () => ({
    useTranslation: () => ({
        t: (k: string) => k,
        i18n: { language: 'en' },
    }),
}));

const mockStartOAuthFlow = vi.fn();

const setupElectronAPI = () => {
    Object.defineProperty(window, 'electronAPI', {
        writable: true,
        value: {
            auth: {
                startOAuthFlow: mockStartOAuthFlow,
            },
        },
    });
};

// Dynamically import AFTER mocks are wired
let OAuthSignInButton: typeof import('./OAuthSignInButton').OAuthSignInButton;

beforeEach(async () => {
    vi.clearAllMocks();
    setupElectronAPI();
    const mod = await import('./OAuthSignInButton');
    OAuthSignInButton = mod.OAuthSignInButton;
});

describe('OAuthSignInButton', () => {
    const onSuccess = vi.fn();
    const onError = vi.fn();

    it('renders with google label and provider icon', () => {
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        expect(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i })).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('renders with microsoft label', () => {
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="microsoft" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        expect(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i })).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('calls startOAuthFlow with correct provider on click', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: true, accountId: 'acc-1' });
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        expect(mockStartOAuthFlow).toHaveBeenCalledWith({ provider: 'google' });
    });

    it('shows spinner and signing-in label while in-flight', async () => {
        let resolveFlow!: (v: unknown) => void;
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockReturnValueOnce(
            new Promise(res => { resolveFlow = res; })
        );
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(screen.getByText('oauth.button.signing-in')).toBeInTheDocument();
        });
        // Button is disabled during flight
        expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toBeDisabled();
        resolveFlow({ success: true, accountId: 'acc-1' });
    });

    it('calls onSuccess with accountId and classifiedProvider on success', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({
            success: true,
            accountId: 'acc-42',
            classifiedProvider: 'microsoft_personal',
        });
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="microsoft" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i }));
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(onSuccess).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
                accountId: 'acc-42',
                classifiedProvider: 'microsoft_personal',
            });
        });
    });

    it('calls onError with error string on failure result', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({
            success: false,
            error: 'user_cancelled',
        });
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(onError).toHaveBeenCalledWith('user_cancelled');
        });
        expect(onSuccess).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('calls onError when startOAuthFlow rejects (thrown error)', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockRejectedValueOnce(new Error('IPC timeout'));
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(onError).toHaveBeenCalledWith('IPC timeout');
        });
    });

    it('does not call startOAuthFlow when disabled prop is set', async () => {
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} disabled />
        );
        const btn = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i });
        expect(btn).toBeDisabled();
        await userEvent.click(btn);
        expect(mockStartOAuthFlow).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('restores idle state after successful flow completes', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: true, accountId: 'acc-1' });
        render(
            <OAuthSignInButton provider="google" onSuccess={onSuccess} onError={onError} />
        );
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        await waitFor(() => expect(onSuccess).toHaveBeenCalled());
        // After success the label should revert (parent typically unmounts the button,
        // but if it doesn't, idle state must be restored)
        expect(screen.queryByText('oauth.button.signing-in')).not.toBeInTheDocument();
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Create `OAuthSignInButton.tsx`**

Create `src/components/OAuthSignInButton.tsx`:

```tsx
import { useState, type FC } from 'react';
import { Loader } from 'lucide-react';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import styles from './OAuthSignInButton.module.css';

// Brand SVG logos inlined so no external dependency is needed.
// Google and Microsoft logos are used per their respective brand guidelines
// for "Sign in with" buttons.

const GoogleLogo: FC<{ size?: number }> = ({ size = 18 }) => (
    <svg
        width={size}
        height={size}
        viewBox="0 0 18 18"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        aria-hidden="true"
    >
        <path
            d="M17.64 9.205c0-.639-.057-1.252-.164-1.841H9v3.481h4.844a4.14 4.14 0 0 1-1.796 2.716v2.259h2.908c1.702-1.567 2.684-3.875 2.684-6.615z"
            fill="#4285F4"
        />
        <path
            d="M9 18c2.43 0 4.467-.806 5.956-2.18l-2.908-2.259c-.806.54-1.837.86-3.048.86-2.344 0-4.328-1.584-5.036-3.711H.957v2.332A8.997 8.997 0 0 0 9 18z"
            fill="#34A853"
        />
        <path
            d="M3.964 10.71A5.41 5.41 0 0 1 3.682 9c0-.593.102-1.17.282-1.71V4.958H.957A8.996 8.996 0 0 0 0 9c0 1.452.348 2.827.957 4.042l3.007-2.332z"
            fill="#FBBC05"
        />
        <path
            d="M9 3.58c1.321 0 2.508.454 3.44 1.345l2.582-2.58C13.463.891 11.426 0 9 0A8.997 8.997 0 0 0 .957 4.958L3.964 7.29C4.672 5.163 6.656 3.58 9 3.58z"
            fill="#EA4335"
        />
    </svg>
);

const MicrosoftLogo: FC<{ size?: number }> = ({ size = 18 }) => (
    <svg
        width={size}
        height={size}
        viewBox="0 0 21 21"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        aria-hidden="true"
    >
        <path d="M10 0H0v10h10V0z" fill="#F25022" />
        <path d="M21 0H11v10h10V0z" fill="#7FBA00" />
        <path d="M10 11H0v10h10V11z" fill="#00A4EF" />
        <path d="M21 11H11v10h10V11z" fill="#FFB900" />
    </svg>
);

export interface OAuthSignInResult {
    accountId: string;
    classifiedProvider?: 'microsoft_personal' | 'microsoft_business';
}

export interface OAuthSignInButtonProps {
    provider: 'google' | 'microsoft';
    onSuccess: (result: OAuthSignInResult) => void;
    onError: (err: string) => void;
    disabled?: boolean;
}

export const OAuthSignInButton: FC<OAuthSignInButtonProps> = ({
    provider,
    onSuccess,
    onError,
    disabled = false,
}) => {
    const { t } = useTranslation();
    const [inFlight, setInFlight] = useState(false);

    const labelKey = provider === 'google'
        ? 'oauth.button.google'
        : 'oauth.button.microsoft';

    const handleClick = async () => {
        if (inFlight || disabled) return;
        setInFlight(true);
        try {
            const electronAPI = (window as unknown as {
                electronAPI?: {
                    auth: {
                        startOAuthFlow: (args: { provider: string }) => Promise<{
                            success: boolean;
                            accountId?: string;
                            classifiedProvider?: 'microsoft_personal' | 'microsoft_business';
                            error?: string;
                        }>;
                    };
                };
            }).electronAPI;

            const result = await electronAPI!.auth.startOAuthFlow({ provider });

            if (result.success && result.accountId) {
                onSuccess({
                    accountId: result.accountId,
                    classifiedProvider: result.classifiedProvider,
                });
            } else {
                onError(result.error ?? 'oauth_failed');
            }
        } catch (err) {
            onError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
        } finally {
            setInFlight(false);
        }
    };

    const isDisabled = disabled || inFlight;
    const Logo = provider === 'google' ? GoogleLogo : MicrosoftLogo;
    const brandClass = provider === 'google'
        ? styles['oauth-btn--google']
        : styles['oauth-btn--microsoft'];

    return (
        <button
            type="button"
            className={`${styles['oauth-btn']} ${brandClass} ${isDisabled ? styles['oauth-btn--disabled'] : ''}`}
            onClick={handleClick}
            disabled={isDisabled}
            aria-label={t(inFlight ? 'oauth.button.signing-in' : labelKey)}
        >
            {inFlight ? (
                <Loader size={18} className={styles['oauth-btn__spinner']} aria-hidden="true" />
            ) : (
                <Logo size={18} />
            )}
            <span className={styles['oauth-btn__label']}>
                {t(inFlight ? 'oauth.button.signing-in' : labelKey)}
            </span>
        </button>
    );
};
```

```css
.oauth-btn {

    font-size: 0.9rem;
    font-weight: 500;
    font-family: inherit;
    cursor: pointer;
    transition: background 0.15s ease, box-shadow 0.15s ease, transform 0.1s ease;
    justify-content: center;

    border-color: rgba(0, 120, 212, 0.45);

    border-color: rgba(0, 120, 212, 0.75);

    opacity: 0.55;

}

    flex: 1;

    animation: oauth-spin 0.9s linear infinite;
    flex-shrink: 0;
}

    from { transform: rotate(0deg); }
    to { transform: rotate(360deg); }
}

@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
    .oauth-btn__spinner {
        animation: none;
    }
}
```

```tsx
// ---- Phase 2 OAuth tests ----

const mockStartOAuthFlow = vi.fn();
const mockAccountsAdd = vi.fn();

// Extend the existing ipcInvoke mock to handle accounts:add
// (the existing mock already stubs 'accounts:test' for password flow tests)

describe('OnboardingScreen — Phase 2 OAuth flows', () => {
    const mockElectronAPI = {
        auth: { startOAuthFlow: mockStartOAuthFlow },
    };

    beforeEach(() => {
        vi.clearAllMocks();
        Object.defineProperty(window, 'electronAPI', {
            writable: true,
            value: mockElectronAPI,
        });
    });

    it('Gmail credentials step renders both OAuth button and password section', async () => {
        const { getByRole, getByLabelText } = render(
            <OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />
        );
        // Navigate: welcome → provider → pick gmail
        await userEvent.click(getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));

            getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
        // Password divider must be present
        expect(screen.getByText('oauth.divider.orUseAppPassword')).toBeInTheDocument();
        // Password field must also be present
        expect(getByLabelText(/settings\.password/i)).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('clicking Gmail OAuth button calls startOAuthFlow with provider=google', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: false, error: 'cancelled' });
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        await userEvent.click(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        expect(mockStartOAuthFlow).toHaveBeenCalledWith({ provider: 'google' });
    });

    it('Gmail OAuth success calls accounts:add with oauth params and invokes onAccountAdded', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({
            success: true,
            accountId: 'new-acc-123',
        });
        const onAccountAdded = vi.fn();
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={onAccountAdded} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        await userEvent.click(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        await waitFor(() => expect(onAccountAdded).toHaveBeenCalled());
    });

    it('outlook-personal card is no longer disabled and shows OAuth button', async () => {
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        // Provider card should exist and be clickable (not disabled)
        const outlookCard = await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /outlook\.com.*personal/i });
        expect(outlookCard).not.toBeDisabled();
        await userEvent.click(outlookCard);
        // OAuth button for microsoft must be shown
        expect(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
        // Coming-soon message must NOT be shown
        expect(screen.queryByText(/oauth2.*not supported/i)).not.toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('outlook-business card shows OAuth button when selected', async () => {
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        const businessCard = await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /microsoft 365/i });
        await userEvent.click(businessCard);
        expect(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('Microsoft classification mismatch shows warning dialog', async () => {
        // User selects outlook-personal but Microsoft returns microsoft_business
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({
            success: true,
            accountId: 'acc-biz',
            classifiedProvider: 'microsoft_business',
        });
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        await userEvent.click(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /outlook\.com.*personal/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i }));
        // Mismatch warning should appear
        expect(
            await screen.findByText(/oauth\.mismatch\.personalSelectedBusinessDetected/i)
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('cancelling during OAuth flow returns to provider card step', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: false, error: 'user_cancelled' });
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        await userEvent.click(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        // After cancelled error the credentials step is still visible (not navigated away)
        await waitFor(() => {
            // Error message shown to user
            expect(screen.getByRole('alert')).toBeInTheDocument();
        });
    });

    it('OAuth error in Gmail flow shows error alert', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: false, error: 'server_error' });
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        await userEvent.click(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i }));
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(screen.getByRole('alert')).toBeInTheDocument();
        });
    });

    it('back button from OAuth credentials step returns to provider grid', async () => {
        render(<OnboardingScreen onAccountAdded={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /get started/i }));
        await userEvent.click(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /outlook\.com.*personal/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /onboarding\.back/i }));
        // Provider grid should be visible again
        expect(await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i })).toBeInTheDocument();
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Modify `OnboardingScreen.tsx` — import OAuthSignInButton and add mismatch state**

In `src/components/OnboardingScreen.tsx`, add the following imports (after the existing imports):

```tsx
import { OAuthSignInButton } from './OAuthSignInButton';
import type { OAuthSignInResult } from './OAuthSignInButton';
```

Add state variables after the existing `useState` declarations (after line 43, before the `useEffect`):

```tsx
const [oauthMismatch, setOauthMismatch] = useState<{
    accountId: string;
    selected: string;
    detected: 'microsoft_personal' | 'microsoft_business';
} | null>(null);
const [oauthSaving, setOauthSaving] = useState(false);
```

- [ ] **Step 5: Add `handleOAuthSuccess` function in `OnboardingScreen.tsx`**

Add after `handleCredentialsNext` (around line 138):

```tsx
const handleOAuthSuccess = async (
    result: OAuthSignInResult,
    selectedProviderId: string
) => {
    // Check for personal/business mismatch on Microsoft flows
    if (
        result.classifiedProvider &&
        selectedProviderId === 'outlook-personal' &&
        result.classifiedProvider === 'microsoft_business'
    ) {
        setOauthMismatch({
            accountId: result.accountId,
            selected: selectedProviderId,
            detected: result.classifiedProvider,
        });
        return;
    }
    if (
        result.classifiedProvider &&
        selectedProviderId === 'outlook-business' &&
        result.classifiedProvider === 'microsoft_personal'
    ) {
        setOauthMismatch({
            accountId: result.accountId,
            selected: selectedProviderId,
            detected: result.classifiedProvider,
        });
        return;
    }
    // No mismatch — commit
    await completeOAuthAdd(result.accountId);
};

const completeOAuthAdd = async (accountId: string) => {
    setOauthSaving(true);
    try {
        // The account was already persisted by the main process during the OAuth flow.
        // We only need to hydrate the store and call the completion callback.
        addAccount({
            id: accountId,
            email: '',          // will be populated by the next accounts:list refresh
            provider: selectedPreset?.id ?? 'gmail',
            display_name: null,
            imap_host: selectedPreset?.imapHost ?? '',
            imap_port: selectedPreset?.imapPort ?? 993,
            smtp_host: selectedPreset?.smtpHost ?? '',
            smtp_port: selectedPreset?.smtpPort ?? 465,
            signature_html: null,
        });
        onAccountAdded();
    } catch {
        showError(t('onboarding.addFailed'));
    } finally {
        setOauthSaving(false);
    }
};
```

- [ ] **Step 6: Modify the `credentials` step render in `OnboardingScreen.tsx`**

Locate the credentials step block — the outer conditional currently checks `selectedPreset.authModel === 'oauth2-required'` (around line 234). Replace that entire conditional with:

```tsx
{/* OAuth-only providers (Outlook personal/business): show OAuth button only */}
{selectedPreset.authModel === 'oauth2-required' && (
    <>
        {oauthMismatch && (
            <div className={styles['ob-error']} role="alert">
                {t(
                    oauthMismatch.detected === 'microsoft_business'
                        ? 'oauth.mismatch.personalSelectedBusinessDetected'
                        : 'oauth.mismatch.businessSelectedPersonalDetected'
                )}
                <div className={styles['ob-mismatch-actions']}>
                    <button
                        className={styles['ob-secondary-btn']}
                        onClick={() => setOauthMismatch(null)}
                    >
                        {t('oauth.mismatch.cancel')}
                    </button>
                    <button
                        className={`${styles['ob-primary-btn']} ${styles['ob-shimmer-btn']}`}
                        onClick={() => {
                            const id = oauthMismatch.accountId;
                            setOauthMismatch(null);
                            completeOAuthAdd(id);
                        }}
                        disabled={oauthSaving}
                    >
                        {t('oauth.mismatch.proceedAnyway')}
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        )}
        {!oauthMismatch && error && (
            <div key={errorKey} className={styles['ob-error']} role="alert">
                {error}
            </div>
        )}
        <OAuthSignInButton
            provider="microsoft"
            onSuccess={(r) => handleOAuthSuccess(r, selectedPreset.id)}
            onError={(err) => showError(err)}
            disabled={oauthSaving}
        />
        <div className={styles['ob-actions']}>
            <button className={styles['ob-secondary-btn']} onClick={() => setStep('provider')}>
                <ChevronLeft size={16} />
                <span>{t('onboarding.back')}</span>
            </button>
        </div>
    </>
)}

{/* Password-supported providers (Gmail, Yahoo, iCloud): dual-path */}
{selectedPreset.authModel !== 'oauth2-required' && selectedPreset.id !== 'custom' && (
    <>
        {error && (
            <div key={errorKey} className={styles['ob-error']} role="alert">
                {error}
            </div>
        )}

        {/* Gmail gets the OAuth button above the divider */}
        {selectedPreset.id === 'gmail' && (
            <>
                <OAuthSignInButton
                    provider="google"
                    onSuccess={(r) => handleOAuthSuccess(r, selectedPreset.id)}
                    onError={(err) => showError(err)}
                    disabled={saving || oauthSaving}
                />
                <div className={styles['ob-oauth-divider']}>
                    <span>{t('oauth.divider.orUseAppPassword')}</span>
                </div>
            </>
        )}

        <div className={styles['ob-form-group']}>
            <label className={styles['ob-label']} htmlFor="ob-email">{t('settings.email')}</label>
            <input
                id="ob-email"
                type="email"
                className={styles['ob-input']}
                placeholder="you@example.com"
                value={email}
                onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                autoFocus
            />
        </div>

        <div className={styles['ob-form-group']}>
            <label className={styles['ob-label']} htmlFor="ob-display-name">
                {t('settings.displayName')} <span className={styles['ob-label-optional']}>{t('onboarding.optional')}</span>
            </label>
            <input
                id="ob-display-name"
                type="text"
                className={styles['ob-input']}
                placeholder="John Doe"
                value={displayName}
                onChange={e => setDisplayName(e.target.value)}
            />
        </div>

        <div className={styles['ob-form-group']}>
            <label className={styles['ob-label']} htmlFor="ob-password">{t('settings.password')}</label>
            <div className={styles['ob-password-wrap']}>
                <input
                    id="ob-password"
                    type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                    className={styles['ob-input']}
                    placeholder="App Password"
                    value={password}
                    onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                />
                <button
                    className={styles['ob-pw-toggle']}
                    onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                    type="button"
                    aria-label={showPassword ? t('onboarding.hidePassword') : t('onboarding.showPassword')}
                >
                    {showPassword ? <EyeOff size={16} /> : <Eye size={16} />}
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div className={styles['ob-actions']}>
            <button className={styles['ob-secondary-btn']} onClick={() => setStep('provider')}>
                <ChevronLeft size={16} />
                <span>{t('onboarding.back')}</span>
            </button>
            <button className={`${styles['ob-primary-btn']} ${styles['ob-shimmer-btn']}`} onClick={handleCredentialsNext} disabled={saving}>
                <span>{saving ? (testStatus === 'testing' ? t('onboarding.testingConnection') : t('onboarding.connecting')) : selectedPreset.id === 'custom' ? t('onboarding.next') : t('onboarding.connect')}</span>
                <ChevronRight size={18} />
            </button>
        </div>
    </>
)}

{/* Custom / server step path — password flow unchanged */}
{selectedPreset.id === 'custom' && (
    <>
        {error && (
            <div key={errorKey} className={styles['ob-error']} role="alert">
                {error}
            </div>
        )}
        <div className={styles['ob-form-group']}>
            <label className={styles['ob-label']} htmlFor="ob-email">{t('settings.email')}</label>
            <input
                id="ob-email"
                type="email"
                className={styles['ob-input']}
                placeholder="you@example.com"
                value={email}
                onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                autoFocus
            />
        </div>
        <div className={styles['ob-form-group']}>
            <label className={styles['ob-label']} htmlFor="ob-display-name">
                {t('settings.displayName')} <span className={styles['ob-label-optional']}>{t('onboarding.optional')}</span>
            </label>
            <input
                id="ob-display-name"
                type="text"
                className={styles['ob-input']}
                placeholder="John Doe"
                value={displayName}
                onChange={e => setDisplayName(e.target.value)}
            />
        </div>
        <div className={styles['ob-form-group']}>
            <label className={styles['ob-label']} htmlFor="ob-password">{t('settings.password')}</label>
            <div className={styles['ob-password-wrap']}>
                <input
                    id="ob-password"
                    type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                    className={styles['ob-input']}
                    placeholder="App Password"
                    value={password}
                    onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                />
                <button
                    className={styles['ob-pw-toggle']}
                    onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                    type="button"
                    aria-label={showPassword ? t('onboarding.hidePassword') : t('onboarding.showPassword')}
                >
                    {showPassword ? <EyeOff size={16} /> : <Eye size={16} />}
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div className={styles['ob-actions']}>
            <button className={styles['ob-secondary-btn']} onClick={() => setStep('provider')}>
                <ChevronLeft size={16} />
                <span>{t('onboarding.back')}</span>
            </button>
            <button className={`${styles['ob-primary-btn']} ${styles['ob-shimmer-btn']}`} onClick={handleCredentialsNext} disabled={saving}>
                <span>{saving ? (testStatus === 'testing' ? t('onboarding.testingConnection') : t('onboarding.connecting')) : t('onboarding.next')}</span>
                <ChevronRight size={18} />
            </button>
        </div>
    </>
)}
```

Add the following CSS to `src/components/OnboardingScreen.module.css` (append at the end of the file):

```css
.ob-oauth-divider {
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    gap: 10px;
    margin: 14px 0;
    color: var(--text-secondary);
    font-size: 0.78rem;
    text-transform: uppercase;
    letter-spacing: 0.06em;
}

.ob-oauth-divider::before,
.ob-oauth-divider::after {
    content: '';
    flex: 1;
    height: 1px;
    background: var(--border-color, rgba(128, 128, 128, 0.25));
}

.ob-mismatch-actions {
    display: flex;
    gap: 8px;
    margin-top: 10px;
    justify-content: flex-end;
}
```

- [ ] **Step 1: Read the existing SettingsModal test mock setup**

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing tests**

Append to `src/components/SettingsModal.test.tsx`:

```tsx
// ---- Phase 2 OAuth add-account tests ----

describe('SettingsModal — Phase 2 OAuth add-account flow', () => {
    const mockStartOAuthFlow = vi.fn();

    const setupOAuthAPI = () => {
        Object.defineProperty(window, 'electronAPI', {
            writable: true,
            value: {
                auth: { startOAuthFlow: mockStartOAuthFlow },
            },
        });
    };

    beforeEach(() => {
        vi.clearAllMocks();
        setupOAuthAPI();
    });

    it('Add Account shows OAuthSignInButton for Gmail preset', async () => {
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        // Navigate to accounts sub-tab and open add account
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i }));
        // Select Gmail provider chip
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        // OAuth button should appear
        expect(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('Add Account shows OAuthSignInButton for outlook-personal preset', async () => {
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /outlook\.com.*personal/i }));
        expect(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('Add Account shows OAuthSignInButton for outlook-business preset', async () => {
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /microsoft 365/i }));
        expect(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.microsoft/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('clicking Gmail OAuth button calls startOAuthFlow with provider=google', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: false, error: 'cancelled' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i })
        );
        expect(mockStartOAuthFlow).toHaveBeenCalledWith({ provider: 'google' });
    });

    it('OAuth success closes the add-account form (resets to list view)', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({
            success: true,
            accountId: 'new-oauth-acc',
        });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i })
        );
        await waitFor(() => {
            // After success the add-account form should be gone and "Add Account" button visible again
            expect(
                screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i })
            ).toBeInTheDocument();
        });
    });

    it('OAuth error shows toast (formError alert)', async () => {
        mockStartOAuthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: false, error: 'network_error' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /settings\.addAccount/i }));
        await userEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /gmail/i }));
        await userEvent.click(
            await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.button\.google/i })
        );
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(screen.getByRole('alert')).toBeInTheDocument();
        });
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Modify `SettingsModal.tsx` — import OAuthSignInButton and add OAuth handler**

```tsx
import { OAuthSignInButton } from './OAuthSignInButton';
import type { OAuthSignInResult } from './OAuthSignInButton';
```

Add the following handler function after `handleUpdateAccount` (around line 643):

```tsx
const handleOAuthAddSuccess = async (result: OAuthSignInResult) => {
    try {
        // Account was persisted by main process during OAuth flow.
        // Hydrate the store and reset the form.
        addAccount({
            id: result.accountId,
            email: '',
            provider: selectedPreset?.id ?? 'gmail',
            display_name: null,
            imap_host: selectedPreset?.imapHost ?? '',
            imap_port: selectedPreset?.imapPort ?? 993,
            smtp_host: selectedPreset?.smtpHost ?? '',
            smtp_port: selectedPreset?.smtpPort ?? 465,
            signature_html: null,
        });
        resetForm();
    } catch {
        setFormError(t('settings.addAccountFailed'));
    }
};

const handleOAuthAddError = (err: string) => {
    setFormError(err);
};
```

- [ ] **Step 5: Replace the `isOAuth2Gated` block in SettingsModal's account form**

Locate the `isOAuth2Gated` conditional in the account form (around line 891). Replace:

```tsx
            </div>

            <div className={styles['form-spacer']} />
            <button className={styles['secondary-btn']} onClick={resetForm}>{t('settings.cancel')}</button>
            <button
                className={styles['secondary-btn']}
                onClick={selectCustomFallback}
                type="button"
            >
                {t('onboarding.useCustomInstead')}
            </button>
        </div>
    </>
) : (
```

with:

```tsx

    <>
        <OAuthSignInButton
            provider={
                selectedPreset?.id === 'gmail'
                    ? 'google'
                    : 'microsoft'
            }
            onSuccess={handleOAuthAddSuccess}
            onError={handleOAuthAddError}
        />
        <div className={styles['form-actions']}>
            <div className={styles['form-spacer']} />
            <button className={styles['secondary-btn']} onClick={resetForm}>{t('settings.cancel')}</button>
            <button
                className={styles['secondary-btn']}
                onClick={selectCustomFallback}
                type="button"
            >
                {t('onboarding.useCustomInstead')}
            </button>
        </div>
    </>
) : (
    <>
        {/* Gmail add-account: show OAuth button above password fields */}
        {!isEditing && selectedPreset?.id === 'gmail' && (
            <>
                <OAuthSignInButton
                    provider="google"
                    onSuccess={handleOAuthAddSuccess}
                    onError={handleOAuthAddError}
```

## Task 22: SettingsModal edit account "Sign in again" CTA

**Files:**
- Modify: `src/components/SettingsModal.tsx`
- Extend: `src/components/SettingsModal.test.tsx`

**Spec references:** D2.7, D11.5b

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing tests**

Append to `src/components/SettingsModal.test.tsx`:

```tsx
// ---- Phase 2 re-auth / edit-account tests ----

describe('SettingsModal — Phase 2 edit-account re-auth CTA', () => {
    const mockGetState = vi.fn();
    const mockStartReauthFlow = vi.fn();

    const setupReauthAPI = () => {
        Object.defineProperty(window, 'electronAPI', {
            writable: true,
            value: {
                auth: {
                    getState: mockGetState,
                    startReauthFlow: mockStartReauthFlow,
                },
            },
        });
    };

    const OAUTH_ACCOUNT = {
        id: 'acc-oauth-1',
        email: 'user@gmail.com',
        provider: 'gmail',
        auth_type: 'oauth2',
        display_name: null,
        imap_host: 'imap.gmail.com',
        imap_port: 993,
        smtp_host: 'smtp.gmail.com',
        smtp_port: 465,
        signature_html: null,
    };

    const LEGACY_OUTLOOK_ACCOUNT = {
        id: 'acc-legacy-1',
        email: 'user@outlook.com',
        provider: 'outlook',
        auth_type: 'password',
        display_name: null,
        imap_host: 'outlook.office365.com',
        imap_port: 993,
        smtp_host: 'smtp.office365.com',
        smtp_port: 587,
        signature_html: null,
    };

    beforeEach(() => {
        vi.clearAllMocks();
        setupReauthAPI();
    });

    it('shows re-auth banner when getState returns needs_reauth', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'needs_reauth' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />, {
            // Provide account in store via wrapper or assume the existing mock adds it
        });
        // Open edit for the oauth account
        // (Assumes the account list renders the account and clicking opens edit mode)
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(OAUTH_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        expect(
            await screen.findByText('oauth.reauth.bannerTitle')
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
        expect(
            screen.getByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.reauth\.cta/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('shows re-auth banner when getState returns recommended_reauth', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'recommended_reauth' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(OAUTH_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        expect(
            await screen.findByText('oauth.reauth.bannerTitle')
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('does NOT show re-auth banner when getState returns ok', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'ok' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(OAUTH_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(mockGetState).toHaveBeenCalled();
        });
        expect(screen.queryByText('oauth.reauth.bannerTitle')).not.toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('clicking Sign in again calls startReauthFlow with accountId', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'needs_reauth' });
        mockStartReauthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: true });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(OAUTH_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        const reauthBtn = await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.reauth\.cta/i });
        await userEvent.click(reauthBtn);
        expect(mockStartReauthFlow).toHaveBeenCalledWith({ accountId: OAUTH_ACCOUNT.id });
    });

    it('password field is hidden for oauth accounts (shows signed-in text instead)', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'ok' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(OAUTH_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        await waitFor(() => expect(mockGetState).toHaveBeenCalled());
        expect(screen.queryByLabelText(/settings\.password/i)).not.toBeInTheDocument();
        expect(screen.getByText(/oauth\.edit\.signedInVia/i)).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('shows legacy Outlook warning banner for auth_type=password provider=outlook', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'recommended_reauth' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(LEGACY_OUTLOOK_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        expect(
            await screen.findByText('oauth.reauth.legacyOutlookWarning')
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('reauth success dismisses the banner', async () => {
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'needs_reauth' });
        mockStartReauthFlow.mockResolvedValueOnce({ success: true });
        // Second call to getState after re-auth resolves with ok
        mockGetState.mockResolvedValueOnce({ state: 'ok' });
        render(<SettingsModal onClose={vi.fn()} />);
        const accountItem = await screen.findByRole('button', {
            name: new RegExp(OAUTH_ACCOUNT.email, 'i'),
        });
        await userEvent.click(accountItem);
        const reauthBtn = await screen.findByRole('button', { name: /oauth\.reauth\.cta/i });
        await userEvent.click(reauthBtn);
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(screen.queryByText('oauth.reauth.bannerTitle')).not.toBeInTheDocument();
        });
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run the failing tests**

Run: `npx vitest run src/components/SettingsModal.test.tsx -t "Phase 2 edit-account re-auth"`

Expected: FAIL — `getState` not called, banner not rendered, password field still present for oauth accounts.

```tsx
// Re-auth state for edit mode
const [reauthState, setReauthState] = useState<'ok' | 'needs_reauth' | 'recommended_reauth' | 'revoked' | null>(null);
const [reauthLoading, setReauthLoading] = useState(false);
```

- [ ] **Step 5: Load reauth state when entering edit mode**

In `enterEditMode`, after the existing `setSelectedPreset` call (around line 520), add:

```tsx
// Load auth state for re-auth banner
setReauthState(null);
const electronAPI = (window as unknown as {
    electronAPI?: {
        auth?: {
            getState: (args: { accountId: string }) => Promise<{ state: string }>;
        };
    };
}).electronAPI;
if (electronAPI?.auth?.getState) {
    electronAPI.auth.getState({ accountId: account.id }).then(res => {
        const s = res.state as 'ok' | 'needs_reauth' | 'recommended_reauth' | 'revoked';
        setReauthState(s);
    }).catch(() => {
        setReauthState('ok'); // Safe default: no banner on IPC failure
    });
}
```

- [ ] **Step 6: Add re-auth banner and password-field suppression to the account form**

In `SettingsModal.tsx`, locate the edit-account form section that renders the password field (around line 952). Wrap the password field `<div className={styles['form-group']}>` block and the re-auth banner, adding them before the existing email `<div className={styles['form-group']}>`:

```tsx
{/* Re-auth banner — shown when getState indicates action needed */}
{isEditing && (reauthState === 'needs_reauth' || reauthState === 'recommended_reauth' || reauthState === 'revoked') && (
    <div className={styles['reauth-banner']} role="alert">
        <div className={styles['reauth-banner__body']}>
            <span className={styles['reauth-banner__title']}>
                {t('oauth.reauth.bannerTitle')}
            </span>
            {editingOriginalProvider === 'outlook' && (
                <span className={styles['reauth-banner__sub']}>
                    {t('oauth.reauth.legacyOutlookWarning')}
                </span>
            )}
        </div>
        <button
            type="button"
            className={styles['reauth-cta-btn']}
            aria-label={t('oauth.reauth.cta')}
            disabled={reauthLoading}
            onClick={async () => {
                if (!editingAccountId) return;
                setReauthLoading(true);
                try {
                    const api = (window as unknown as {
                        electronAPI?: {
                            auth?: {
                                startReauthFlow: (args: { accountId: string }) => Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }>;
                                getState: (args: { accountId: string }) => Promise<{ state: string }>;
                            };
                        };
                    }).electronAPI;
                    const result = await api?.auth?.startReauthFlow({ accountId: editingAccountId });
                    if (result?.success) {
                        const fresh = await api?.auth?.getState({ accountId: editingAccountId });
                        const s = (fresh?.state ?? 'ok') as 'ok' | 'needs_reauth' | 'recommended_reauth' | 'revoked';
                        setReauthState(s);
                    } else {
                        setFormError(result?.error ?? t('oauth.reauth.failed'));
                    }
                } catch {
                    setFormError(t('oauth.reauth.failed'));
                } finally {
                    setReauthLoading(false);
                }
            }}
        >
            {reauthLoading ? <Loader size={14} /> : t('oauth.reauth.cta')}
        </button>
    </div>
)}

{/* Signed-in-via text replaces password field for oauth2 accounts */}
{isEditing && editingAccountForAuthType === 'oauth2' ? (
    <div className={styles['form-group']}>
        <label className={styles['form-label']}>{t('settings.password')}</label>
        <p className={styles['oauth-signed-in-text']}>
            {t('oauth.edit.signedInVia', { provider: selectedPreset?.label ?? '' })}
        </p>
    </div>
) : (
    <div className={styles['form-group']}>
        <label className={styles['form-label']} htmlFor="settings-password">{t('settings.password')}</label>
        <div className={styles['password-wrapper']}>
            <input
                id="settings-password"
                type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                className={styles['form-input']}
                placeholder={isEditing ? t('settings.passwordKeep') : t('settings.passwordNew')}
                value={formPassword}
                onChange={e => { setFormPassword(e.target.value); resetTestStatus(); }}
            />
            <button
                className={styles['password-toggle']}
                onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                type="button"
                aria-label={showPassword ? t('settings.hidePassword') : t('settings.showPassword')}
            >
                {showPassword ? <EyeOff size={16} /> : <Eye size={16} />}
            </button>
        </div>
    </div>
)}
```

Add the `editingAccountForAuthType` derived value near the top of the render function (after the existing `isEditing` declaration, around line 705):

```tsx
const editingAccountForAuthType = isEditing
    ? (accounts.find(a => a.id === editingAccountId)?.auth_type ?? 'password')
    : 'password';
```

```tsx
// ---- Phase 2 reauth indicator tests ----

describe('Sidebar — Phase 2 reauth indicators', () => {
    const mockOnNeedsReauth = vi.fn();
    const mockSetAccounts = vi.fn();

    const setupReauthAPI = () => {
        Object.defineProperty(window, 'electronAPI', {
            writable: true,
            value: {
                auth: { onNeedsReauth: mockOnNeedsReauth },
            },
        });
    };

        },

            id: 'acc-recommended',
            email: 'legacy@outlook.com',
            provider: 'outlook',
            auth_type: 'password',
            auth_state: 'recommended_reauth',
            display_name: 'Recommended Reauth',
            imap_host: 'outlook.office365.com',
            imap_port: 993,
            smtp_host: 'smtp.office365.com',
            smtp_port: 587,
            signature_html: null,
        },
    ];

    beforeEach(() => {
        vi.clearAllMocks();
        setupReauthAPI();
        // Return a no-op cleanup for onNeedsReauth listener
        mockOnNeedsReauth.mockReturnValue(() => {});
    });

    it('renders amber alert badge for recommended_reauth account', async () => {
        render(<Sidebar onCompose={vi.fn()} onSettings={vi.fn()} />, {
            // Feed ACCOUNTS_WITH_REAUTH via store wrapper in test
        });
        // The badge next to 'Recommended Reauth' (or 'legacy@outlook.com') should have amber styling
        const badge = await screen.findByTitle('oauth.reauth.badge.recommended');
        expect(badge).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('renders red alert badge for needs_reauth account', async () => {
        render(<Sidebar onCompose={vi.fn()} onSettings={vi.fn()} />);
        const badge = await screen.findByTitle('oauth.reauth.badge.needed');
        expect(badge).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

        // Wait for the ok account to be rendered

        // No badge for ok account
        expect(screen.queryByTitle('oauth.reauth.badge.needed')).not.toBeInTheDocument();
        // Note: there will be a badge for the other two accounts, just not for ok
    });

    it('subscribes to auth:needs-reauth event on mount via onNeedsReauth', async () => {
        render(<Sidebar onCompose={vi.fn()} onSettings={vi.fn()} />);
        await waitFor(() => {
            expect(mockOnNeedsReauth).toHaveBeenCalled();
        });
    });

    it('unsubscribes auth:needs-reauth listener on unmount', async () => {
        const mockCleanup = vi.fn();
        mockOnNeedsReauth.mockReturnValueOnce(mockCleanup);
        const { unmount } = render(<Sidebar onCompose={vi.fn()} onSettings={vi.fn()} />);
        await waitFor(() => expect(mockOnNeedsReauth).toHaveBeenCalled());
        unmount();
        expect(mockCleanup).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('account context menu has "Sign in again" item for needs_reauth account', async () => {
        render(<Sidebar onCompose={vi.fn()} onSettings={vi.fn()} />);
        // Right-click or open context menu on the needs-reauth account
        const accountBtn = await screen.findByText('Needs Reauth');
        await userEvent.pointer({ target: accountBtn, keys: '[MouseRight]' });
        expect(
            await screen.findByRole('menuitem', { name: /oauth\.reauth\.contextMenuItem/i })
        ).toBeInTheDocument();
    });

    it('clicking "Sign in again" context menu item calls onSettings', async () => {
        const onSettings = vi.fn();
        render(<Sidebar onCompose={vi.fn()} onSettings={onSettings} />);
        const accountBtn = await screen.findByText('Needs Reauth');
        await userEvent.pointer({ target: accountBtn, keys: '[MouseRight]' });
        const menuItem = await screen.findByRole('menuitem', { name: /oauth\.reauth\.contextMenuItem/i });
        await userEvent.click(menuItem);
        expect(onSettings).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Add alert badge rendering to `Sidebar.tsx`**

Add the following `useEffect` for the `auth:needs-reauth` listener, after the existing MCP status effect (around line 433):

```tsx
// Subscribe to main-process auth:needs-reauth push event (Phase 2)
useEffect(() => {
    const api = (window as unknown as {
        electronAPI?: {
            auth?: {
                onNeedsReauth: (cb: (payload: { accountId: string }) => void) => () => void;
            };
        };
    }).electronAPI;
    if (!api?.auth?.onNeedsReauth) return;
    const unsub = api.auth.onNeedsReauth((payload) => {
        // Refresh account auth_state from DB for the affected account.
        // We trigger a full accounts reload via IPC so the badge updates immediately.
        ipcInvoke<Array<{
            id: string;
            email: string;
            provider: string;
            auth_type?: string;
            auth_state?: string;
            display_name: string | null;
            imap_host: string;
            imap_port: number;
            smtp_host: string;
            smtp_port: number;
            signature_html: string | null;
        }>>('accounts:list').then(result => {
            if (Array.isArray(result)) {
                // Update just the affected account's state in the store
                const updated = result.find(a => a.id === payload.accountId);
                if (updated) {
                    useEmailStore.getState().updateAccount({
                        id: updated.id,
                        email: updated.email,
                        provider: updated.provider,
                        display_name: updated.display_name,
                        imap_host: updated.imap_host,
                        imap_port: updated.imap_port,
                        smtp_host: updated.smtp_host,
                        smtp_port: updated.smtp_port,
                        signature_html: updated.signature_html,
                    });
                }
            }
        }).catch(() => { /* fire-and-forget — badge will refresh on next poll */ });
    });
    return () => { unsub(); };
}, []);
```

## Task 24: ProviderHelpPanel OAuth notes

**Files:**
- Modify: `src/lib/providerPresets.ts`
- Modify: `src/components/ProviderHelpPanel.tsx`
- Extend: `src/components/ProviderHelpPanel.test.tsx`

**Spec references:** D2.9

Updates `providerPresets.ts` to shift `outlook-personal` and `outlook-business` from their Phase 1 `'oauth2-required'` disabled state to `'oauth2-supported'` (OAuth2 is now implemented), with new i18n key references for OAuth-specific panel content. Updates `ProviderHelpPanel.tsx` to render an accent-background OAuth banner for OAuth-supported providers, dual-path sections for Gmail, and a legacy reauth warning for `'legacy'` accounts. Extends the ProviderHelpPanel test file with 6 new tests covering the new render paths.

New i18n keys introduced by this task (all under `oauth.providerHelp.*`):

| Key | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `oauth.providerHelp.bannerTitle` | Accent banner shown for oauth2-supported providers — e.g. "Sign in with {{provider}} for the fastest setup — no app password needed." |
| `oauth.providerHelp.gmailOAuthNote` | Supplemental note under Gmail banner when dual-path is shown |
| `oauth.providerHelp.outlookPersonalOAuthNote` | Supplemental note for Outlook Personal OAuth path |
| `oauth.providerHelp.outlookBusinessOAuthNote` | Supplemental note for Outlook Business OAuth path |
| `oauth.providerHelp.legacyReauthWarning` | Warning text shown in panel for legacy outlook accounts needing reauth |

New preset step keys (under `providerPresets.*`):

| Key | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `providerPresets.gmail.oauthSteps` | Array of steps for the Gmail OAuth path (shown when user prefers app-password instead) |
| `providerPresets.outlookPersonal.oauthSteps` | OAuth setup notes for Outlook personal (informational) |
| `providerPresets.outlookBusiness.oauthSteps` | OAuth setup notes for Outlook business (informational) |

- [ ] **Step 1: Write failing tests in `src/components/ProviderHelpPanel.test.tsx`**
